#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x000E [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x0909)
  1: 0x0011 [0x21] END_EVENT
  2: 0x0012 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()

SUBROUTINE_0909:
  3: 0x0909 [0x1E] EventEntity looks at LocalPlayer and starts talking
  4: 0x090E [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x5872)
```
